   "source": [
    "## O'Reily BP Models\n",
    "\n",
    "Before working with anything close to state of the art (SOTA), a good place to start is with the backpropagation model that O'Reily used in his paper.\n",
    "\n",
    "First, let's create the training and testing data that will be used."
   ]
  },
  {
   "cell_type": "code",
   "execution_count": 47,
   "metadata": {},
   "outputs": [
    {
     "name": "stdout",
     "output_type": "stream",
     "text": [
      "Training X shape: (100, 4, 5, 5). Training y shape: (100, 4, 5, 2)\n",
      "Testing X shape: (500, 4, 5, 5). Testing y shape: (500, 4, 5, 2)\n"
     ]
    }
   ],
   "source": [
    "# Data parameters\n",
    "stack = 4\n",
    "size = 5\n",
    "dims = 2\n",
    "\n",
    "# Training Data\n",
    "training_n = 100\n",
    "training_y = cg.generate_labels(n_samples=training_n, stack=stack, size=size, dims=dims)\n",
    "training_x = cg.inverse_transform(training_y)\n",
    "# Testing data\n",
    "testing_n = 500\n",
    "testing_y = cg.generate_labels(n_samples=testing_n, stack=stack, size=size, dims=dims)\n",
    "testing_x = cg.inverse_transform(testing_y)\n",
    "\n",
    "print('Training X shape: {0}. Training y shape: {1}'.format(training_x.shape, training_y.shape))\n",
    "print('Testing X shape: {0}. Testing y shape: {1}'.format(testing_x.shape, testing_y.shape))"
   ]
  },

   "source": [
    "def bp_model(hidden_units=100, stack=4, size=5, dims=2):\n",
    "    \"\"\"Builds and returns the model\"\"\"\n",
    "    model = models.Sequential()\n",
    "    model.add(layers.Reshape((stack*size*size,), name='Initial_reshape'))\n",
    "    # Single hidden layer\n",
    "    model.add(layers.Dense(hidden_units, activation='sigmoid', name='Hidden_Layer'))\n",
    "    # Output layer\n",
    "    model.add(layers.Dense(stack*size*dims, activation='sigmoid', name='Output_Layer'))\n",
    "    # Reshape to match the labels\n",
    "    model.add(layers.Reshape((stack, size, dims), name='Output_reshape'))\n",
    "    \n",
    "    model.compile(optimizer='rmsprop', \n",
    "                  loss='mse', \n",
    "                  metrics=['accuracy'])\n",
    "    return model\n",
    "\n",
    "model = bp_model()\n",
    "model.fit(training_x, training_y, epochs=500, batch_size=1, verbose=0, callbacks=[TQDMNotebookCallback()])\n",
    "model.summary()\n",
    "\n",
    "score = model.evaluate(testing_x, testing_y, batch_size=1)\n",
    "print('Loss and accuracy:', score)"
   ]

   "source": [
    "def bp_model_tanh(hidden_units=100, stack=4, size=5, dims=2):\n",
    "    \"\"\"Builds and returns the model\"\"\"\n",
    "    model = models.Sequential()\n",
    "    model.add(layers.Reshape((stack*size*size,), name='Initial_reshape'))\n",
    "    # Single hidden layer\n",
    "    model.add(layers.Dense(hidden_units, activation='tanh', name='Hidden_Layer'))\n",
    "    # Output layer\n",
    "    model.add(layers.Dense(stack*size*dims, activation='tanh', name='Output_Layer'))\n",
    "    # Reshape to match the labels\n",
    "    model.add(layers.Reshape((stack, size, dims), name='Output_reshape'))\n",
    "    \n",
    "    model.compile(optimizer='rmsprop', \n",
    "                  loss='mse', \n",
    "                  metrics=['accuracy'])\n",
    "    return model\n",
    "\n",
    "model = bp_model_tanh()\n",
    "model.fit(training_x, training_y, epochs=500, batch_size=1, verbose=0, callbacks=[TQDMNotebookCallback()])\n",
    "model.summary()\n",
    "\n",
    "score = model.evaluate(testing_x, testing_y, batch_size=1)\n",
    "print('Loss and accuracy:', score)\n",
    "\n",
    "example_y = cg.generate_labels()\n",
    "example_x = cg.inverse_transform(example_y)\n",
    "pred_y = model.predict(example_x)\n",
    "cgh.heatmap(pred_y)\n",
    "cgh.heatmap(example_y)\n",
    "plt.show()"
   ]
  },

   "source": [
    "def bp_model_sig_lin(hidden_units=100, stack=4, size=5, dims=2):\n",
    "    \"\"\"Builds and returns the model\"\"\"\n",
    "    model = models.Sequential()\n",
    "    model.add(layers.Reshape((stack*size*size,), name='Initial_reshape'))\n",
    "    # Single hidden layer\n",
    "    model.add(layers.Dense(hidden_units, activation='sigmoid', name='Hidden_Layer'))\n",
    "    # Output layer\n",
    "    model.add(layers.Dense(stack*size*dims, activation=None, name='Output_Layer'))\n",
    "    # Reshape to match the labels\n",
    "    model.add(layers.Reshape((stack, size, dims), name='Output_reshape'))\n",
    "    \n",
    "    model.compile(optimizer='rmsprop', \n",
    "                  loss='mse', \n",
    "                  metrics=['accuracy'])\n",
    "    return model\n",
    "\n",
    "model = bp_model_sig_lin()\n",
    "model.fit(training_x, training_y, epochs=500, batch_size=1, verbose=0, callbacks=[TQDMNotebookCallback()])\n",
    "model.summary()\n",
    "\n",
    "score = model.evaluate(testing_x, testing_y, batch_size=1)\n",
    "print('Loss and accuracy:', score)\n",
    "\n",
    "example_y = cg.generate_labels()\n",
    "example_x = cg.inverse_transform(example_y)\n",
    "pred_y = model.predict(example_x)\n",
    "cgh.heatmap(pred_y)\n",
    "cgh.heatmap(example_y)\n",
    "plt.show()"
   ]
